In answer to the question

тАЬBut this does not mean intermarriage among them “,

they declared that this (prohibition of inter-marriage) is due to caste
and that the praise of the man is due to his possession of virtues.

(They) express the above following conclusion.

En respuesta a la pregunta

“Pero esto no significa matrimonios mixtos entre ellos”,

Declararon que esta (prohibici├│n del matrimonio) se debe a la casta
y que el elogio del hombre se debe a su posesi├│n de virtudes.

(Ellos) expresan lo anterior conclusi├│n.

English

The saying current in the families of those who are exclusively devoted to Bhagav─Бn (ekant─л) is indeed as follows :

“He to whom V─Бsudeva is not the (sole) deity from birth to death
let him not be born into our family
and even if he is born,
let him die soon.”

Espa├▒ol

El dicho actual en las familias de aquellos que est├бn dedicados exclusivamente a Bhagav─Бn (Ekant─л) es de hecho la siguiente:

“Aquel a quien V─Бsudeva no es la deidad (├║nica) desde el nacimiento hasta la muerte
Que no nazca en nuestra familia
e incluso si nace,
D├йjalo morir pronto “.

рдЗрддреНрдпреН рдПрддрд╛рд╡рджреН рдПрд╡ ред

English

In such passages as this:-

“He should be considered as a ┼Ъ┼лdra”,

the great sages called men of higher castes
by the words applicable to the lower castes
and vice versa
merely to indicate the degree of consideration or respect to be shown.

Espa├▒ol

En pasajes como este:-

“Deber├нa ser considerado como un ┼Ъ┼лdra”,

Los grandes sabios llamados hombres de castas superiores
por las palabras aplicables a las castas inferiores y viceversa
simplemente para indicar el grado de consideraci├│n o respeto que se mostrar├б.

English

Therefore the purport of the ┼Ы─Бstra is only this much:

тАЬBrahmins who are not devotees of Bhagav─Бn
are not to be held in esteem,
whereas ┼Ъ┼лdras who are devotees of Bhagav─Бn
should be as much esteemed as Brahmins.”

Espa├▒ol

Por lo tanto, el significado del ┼Ъ─Бstra es solo esto:

тАЬBrahmanes que no son devotos de Bhagav─Бn
no deben ser retenidos en estima
mientras que ┼Ъ┼лdras que son devotos de Bhagav─Бn
Deber├нa ser tan estimado como los brahmanes “.

it is to state that he should be esteemed as such at heart.

English

When this Brahma Jnani (Vidura) gave up his life by the power of yoga,
Dharmaputra (it is true) felt it his duty (as his nephew) to perform his funeral obsequies in the special form (of Brahmamedha tyAga).
But it may have been performed in silence (without mantras;)
or it was justifiable in the case of that exceptional individual. +++(5)+++

Espa├▒ol

Cuando este Brahma Jnani (Vidura) renunci├│ a su vida por el poder del yoga,
Dharmaputra (es cierto) sinti├│ que era su deber (como su sobrino) realizar sus obsequias funerarias en la forma especial (de tyAga).
Pero puede haberse realizado en silencio (sin mantras;)
O era justificable en el caso de ese individuo excepcional.+++(5)+++

English

This should not be considered as a precedent in the case of other individuals (as a principle applicable to all).

Espa├▒ol

Esto no debe considerarse como un precedente en el caso de otras personas (como un principio aplicable a todos).

рдПрд╡рдВ рджреЗрд╡рд╛рдЬреНрдЮрд╛рдГ рдХреНрд╡рдЪрд┐рдЪреН рдЫрд╛рд╕реНрддреНрд░рдореН рдЕрддрд┐рдХреНрд░рдореНрдп +рдЕрд╡рд┐рд╡рджрдиреАрдп-рд╕реНрд╡рдкреНрдирд╛рджрд┐рднрд┐рд░реН рдЕрдкрд┐ рдЬреНрдЮрд╛рдпрдиреНрддреЗред

English

If (this answer) were not accepted,
it would follow that, because the virtuous Pandavas had a common wife,
owing to the force of certain exceptional circumstances,
others, too, might do likewise.
(This would lead to promiscuity in social relations ).

Espa├▒ol

Si (esta respuesta) no fuera aceptado,
Seguir├нa eso, porque los Pandavas virtuosos ten├нan una esposa com├║n,
Debido a la fuerza de ciertas circunstancias excepcionales,
Otros tambi├йn podr├нan hacer lo mismo.
(Esto conducir├нa a la promiscuidad en las relaciones sociales).

рдореВрд▓рдореН

рдиреАрд▓рдореЗрдШрдГ (рд╕рдВ)

рдЕрддрдГ рд╕реНрд╡-рд╕реНрд╡-рдЬрд╛рддреАрд░реН рдЕ-рд╡рд┐рдЬрд╣рджреНрднрд┐рдГ рд╕рджреНрднрд┐рдГ

рдпрдерд╛рд╜рдзрд┐рдХрд╛рд░рдВ рднрдЧрд╡рддреН-рдХреИрдЩреНрдХрд░реНрдпрдВ рдХрд░реНрддреБрдВ рдпреБрдХреНрддрдореН ред

English

Therefore each individual should stand firm in his caste
and render service (kaiс╣Еkarya) to Bhagav─Бn
in accordance with what is prescribed as competent for that caste.

Espa├▒ol

Por lo tanto, cada individuo debe mantenerse firme en su casta
y prender el servicio (Kaiс╣Еkarya) a Bhagav─Бn
de acuerdo con lo que se prescribe como competente para esa casta.

English

Those who abide by the ┼Ы─Бstras should not believe in the elevation from (lower) castes stated in the deceptive ┼Ы─Бstras (of heretics ).

Espa├▒ol

Aquellos que cumplen con los ┼Ъ─Бstras
no deben creer en la elevaci├│n de las castas (m├бs bajas)
declaradas en el enga├▒oso ┼Ъ─Бstras (de los herejes).

[[реирейрек]]

English

The case of such as Visvamitra
(who became a Brahmin after being a Kс╣гatriya),
was due to certain special causes as the charu (oblation of grain cooked in milk and other things)
eaten by his mother without knowing
that it was intended for producing a Brahmin child -
it should not be considered that it is applicable to others as well,
for it is against the texts (in the ┼Ыastras).

Espa├▒ol

El caso de tales como Visvamitra
(que se convirti├│ en brahm├бn despu├йs de ser un kс╣гatriya),
se debi├│ a ciertas causas especiales como el charu (oblaci├│n de grano cocinado en leche y otras cosas)
comido por su madre sin saber
que estaba destinado a producir un ni├▒o brahm├бn -
no debe considerarse que tambi├йn sea aplicable a otros,
porque est├б en contra de los textos (en los ┼Ъastras).

рдиреАрд▓рдореЗрдШрдГ (рд╕рдВ)

[[реирейрем]]

рд╡рд┐рджреБрд░рд╛рджрд┐рднреНрдпреЛ рд╜рдкреНрдпреН рдЙрддреНрдХреГрд╖реНрдЯрдкреНрд░рднрд╛рд╡рд╛рдгрд╛рдВ рджрд┐рд╡реНрдп-рд╕реВрд░реАрдгрд╛рдВ рд╡реГрддреНрддрд╛рдиреНрдд-рд╡рд┐рд╢реЗрд╖рд╛
рдЕрд╕реНрдорджреН-рдЕрдиреБрд╖реНрдард╛рдирд╕реНрдп рди рджреГрд╖реНрдЯрд╛рдиреНрддреА рдХрд╛рд░реНрдпрд╛рдГ ред

English

The incidents and conduct of the Alvars
who were possessed of powers even superior to those of Vidura and others
should not be taken as precedents for our conduct.

Espa├▒ol

Los incidentes y la conducta de los Alvars
a quienes pose├нan poderes incluso superiores a los de Vidura y otros
no debe tomarse como precedentes para nuestra conducta.

If we examine even their conduct carefully,
(we shall find) that they did not transgress the rules of their respective castes.

рдЬреНрдЮрд╛рдирдореН, рд╢рд┐рдХреНрд╖рд╛, рдЬрд╛рддрд┐рдГ

English

The ┼Ыloka :-

“Viс╣гс╣Зu” is always to be praised (in song) with true knowledge (j├▒─Бna).
Therefore the pure knowledge concerning the eternal Lord
should be obtained in clearness
either from Brahmins or from Kс╣гatriyas or from Vai┼Ыyas or from ┼Ъ┼лdras or from even lower castes -

Espa├▒ol

El ┼Ъloka:-

“Viс╣гс╣Зu” siempre es ser alabado (en la canci├│n) con verdadero conocimiento (j├▒─Бna). Por lo tanto, el conocimiento puro sobre el se├▒or eterno debe obtenerse en claridad ya sea de brahmanes o de kс╣гatriyas o de vai┼Ыyas o de ┼Ы┼лdras o de castas incluso inferiores -

рдиреАрд▓рдореЗрдШрдГ (рд╕рдВ)

English

this ┼Ыloka means merely that since knowledge of Bhagav─Бn is essential as an acquisition,
mere knowledge in its clearness should be obtained,
when men of the previous castes are not available,
even from those that are below them.

Espa├▒ol

Cuando los hombres de las castas anteriores no est├бn disponibles,
Incluso de los que est├бn debajo de ellos.

рдиреАрд▓рдореЗрдШрдГ (рд╕рдВ)

рддреБрд▓рд╛-рдзрд╛рд░–рдзрд░реНрдо-рд╡реНрдпрд╛рдзрд╛рджрдпреЛ рд╜рдкрд┐

рддреАрд░реНрде-рдпрд╛рддреНрд░рд╛рдпрд╛рдВ рдорд╛рд░реНрдЧ-рд╕рдиреНрджрд┐рд╣рд╛рдирд╛рдирд╛рдВ рдорд╛рд░реНрдЧреЗ-рдпреЛрдЬрди-рдорд╛рддреНрд░-рдХрд░рдгрд╡рддреН
рддрд╛рдиреН рд╕рдВрдкреНрд░рдмреЛрдзреНрдп рд╡реНрдпрд╕реГрдЬрдиреНрдиреН рдЗрддреНрдпреН рдПрддрд╛рд╡рджреН рдПрд╡ ;
рди рддреБ рдореБрдЦреНрдпрдореН рдЖрдЪрд╛рд░реНрдпрдХрдВ рдЪрдХреНрд░реБрдГ ред

English

Tuladhara and Dharmavyadha (who were of lower castes) only did this much:
they treated with respect the Brahmins who came to them
to have their doubts cleared regarding dharma
and made them understand the points at issue,
just like people who put pilgrims on the right path
when they happen to have lost their way.
They did not become the main ─Бc─Бryas (of the Brahmins).

Espa├▒ol

Tuladhara y Dharmavyadha (que eran de castas inferiores) solo hicieron esto:
trataron con respeto a los brahmanes que vinieron a ellos
tener sus dudas despejadas con respecto al dharma
y les hizo entender los puntos en cuesti├│n,
Al igual que las personas que ponen a los peregrinos en el camino correcto
cuando han perdido su rumbo.
No se convirtieron en el principal ─Бc─Бryas (de los brahmanes).

(рдЧрд╛рд░реБрдб-рдкреБрд░рд╛рдгрдореН)

English

“Bhakti or devotion is of eight kinds.
If this bhakti is found in a mleccha,
he should be considered as a devout and knowing Brahmin.
To him giving is proper and from him taking is proper.
He should be treated with the same reverence as I myself”.

Espa├▒ol

“Bhakti o la devoci├│n son de ocho tipos.
Si este bhakti se encuentra en una mleccha,
Deber├нa ser considerado como un brahm├бn devoto y conocido.
Para ├йl, dar es apropiado
y de ├йl tomar es apropiado.
Deber├нa ser tratado con la misma reverencia que yo mismo “.

рдЗрддрд┐ рдордиреНрджрдореН рдЗрджрдВ рд╡рдЪрдГ рее

English

Therefore the contention that all devotees of Viс╣гс╣Зu are of the same caste
either because of the lower caste perishing or of all castes perishing–
this contention is foolish.

Espa├▒ol

Por lo tanto, la afirmaci├│n de que todos los devotos de Viс╣гс╣Зu son de la misma casta
ya sea por la casta inferior que perec├нa o de todas las castas que perec├нan
Esta afirmaci├│n es tonta.

Reverence for the sake of devotion to Bhagav─Бn is common, according to the sages, to all.

тАШтАШрд╕реНрддреНрд░рд┐рдпреЛ рд╡реИрд╢реНрдпрд╛рд╕реН рддрдерд╛ рд╢реВрджреНрд░рд╛рд╕реН

“Women, Vai┼Ыyas and ┼Ъ┼лdras, even among these,

English

Owing to the preponderance of such qualities as sattvam, in the body,
a man is entitled to be called a Brahmin, a Kс╣гatriya and the like.

рдиреАрд▓рдореЗрдШрдГ (рд╕рдВ)

English

Owing to the Brahmin-like qualities (of the mind) and the like,
the attainment of the supreme end of life and the up─Бyas therefor
and also such things as eulogy may be found in all castes.

el logro del fin de la vida supremo y los up─Бyas por ello

English

If in a Brahmin are found such features as are incongruous (with his caste),
it will meet with censure that,
born in a caste which is declared by the ┼Ъ─Бstras as being capable of such virtues as self restraint and mental serenity,
he lapsed from the condition suitable to him.

(рдпрд╛рдЬреНрдЮрд╡рд▓реНрдХреНрдпрд╕реНрдореГрддрд┐ рез-резрезрем)

рдЗрддреНрдпреН-рдЖрджреНрдпреН-рдЙрдХреНрдд-рд░реАрддреНрдпрд╛

English

If a man born in other castes acquires the higher virtues,
he will be extolled highly as stated in the ┼Ыloka :-

“Men are to be honoured in the following order of preference–
for the possession of vidy─Б (j├▒─Бna), of right karma, of age, of relatives and of wealth.
Even a ┼Ъ┼лdra possessing these is fit to be honoured in old age”.

Espa├▒ol

Ser├б exaltado altamente como se indica en el ┼Ъloka:-

“Los hombres deben ser honrados en el siguiente orden de preferencia
por la posesi├│n de Vidy─Б (j├▒─Бna), del karma derecho, de edad, de familiares y de riqueza.

there is nothing to prevent a person from being honoured in the mind as established above.
